STAT

static font

Variable font must have a STAT table.

Open Sans Condensed Light Regular (OpenSansCondensed-Light.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'OpenSansCondensed-Light', Everything looks good.

Pass

This font software is the property of Monotype Imaging Inc., or one of its affiliated entities (collectively, Monotype) and its use by you is covered under the terms of a license agreement. Unless you have entered into a specific license agreement granting you additional rights, your use of this software is limited by the terms of the actual license agreement you have entered into with Monotype. You may not copy or distribute this software. If you have any questions concerning your rights you should review the license agreement you received with the software. You can learn more about Monotype by clicking here: www.monotype.com.

Open Sans Condensed Light Regular (OpenSansCondensed-Light.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Open Sans Condensed' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Light' = NID 1 'Open Sans Condensed Light'.

Pass

Open Sans Condensed Light Italic (OpenSansCondensed-LightItalic.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'OpenSansCondensed-LightItalic', Everything looks good.

Open Sans Condensed Light Italic (OpenSansCondensed-LightItalic.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Open Sans Condensed' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Light Italic' = NID 1 'Open Sans Condensed Light' + 'Space' + NID 2 'Italic'.

Pass

Open Sans Condensed Bold (OpenSansCondensed-Bold.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'OpenSansCondensed-Bold', Everything looks good.

Pass

Kerning (kern Table and GPOS Kerning)

Kerning (kern Table and GPOS Kerning)

Error

Open Sans Condensed Light Regular (OpenSansCondensed-Light.ttf)

GPOS

kern

Simple check if kern feature in GPOS table.

GPOS table does not have kerning feature. Please investigate if this meets requirements.

Warning

Open Sans Condensed Light Regular (OpenSansCondensed-Light.ttf)

kern

-/-

Check if 'kern' table in TTF font.

Font has 'kern' table. Please verify if font requires kern table or if only GPOS kerning should be in font.
For example: PowerPoint only supports a flat GPOS kerning or a kern table. So, if the customer requires PowerPoint support, a kern table is necessary.
